 5401338 The civic elections will be held on November 16 in Rajasthan
 The results of the civic elections will be held on November 19
 The Congress has split into two factions with the six rebel mlas joining hands with the Bahujan Samaj Party (BSP) in Rajasthan
 party main pro gahalot gut kaa maananaa he ki in netaaon kii vajah se party ko majbootee mili or pradesh vidhansabha main congress ke number bade hai
 Due to which the government got stability and hence these mlas should get ministerial posts
 basapa se congress main shaamil hone vaale vidhayakon ne ajtak se khaas baatcheet main kaha ki pad dena naa dena mukhyamantri, pradesh prabharee ke haath main he
 He says that he has joined the party to work in Congress and for the development of his areas
 lekin yah saaf he kibaspa se aae vidhayakonko lekar congress main gutbaji phir se tej ho gai he
 Legislator Wajib Ali, who left the BSP and joined the Congress, said that the civic elections were in front
 aise main hamen milakar sanghathan ko majboot karke in chunaavon kaa saamana karnaa he
 All these things were considered in the coming times, how the development works of the area are reached
 ham log jaise milakar party main shaamil hue hai, aise hi aane vaale vakt main sab milakar majboot congress kaa saath denge
 What do the leaders of the Sachin Pilot group want? On the other hand, the leaders who are close to the party president and state Deputy Chief Minister Sachin Pilot believe that the leaders already in the party and the long-serving legislators, activists and leaders should get priority
 
 payalat gut kii soch he ki agar gahalot sarkaar kaa mantrimandal kaa vistaar hota he to jo netaa pehle se congress main kaam karte aa rahe hai, unako tavajjo di jaani chahie
 It should not be so that by ignoring them, they should annoy the old party workers by giving them the posts of ministers from outside or in other bodies
 puraane kaaryakartaaon ko mili praathamiktasachin payalat jo pradesh ke upmukhyamantri hone ke saath-saath party ke pradesh congress cameti ke adhyaksh bhi hai, pehle hi saaf taur par kah chuke hai ki jo log party main shaamil hue hai wo bina kisi inaam kii ichha se congress party main aae hai, agar koi vistaar hoti he, to usamen congress ke puraane kaaryakartaaon or netaaon ko praathamikta milani chahie
 These mlas are also attending meetings being held by top Congress leaders before the civic elections
 saath hi bad-chadhakar sanghathan ke liye kaam karne kii baat bhi kar rahe hai
 It is being said that these leaders have been asked by the party to work vigorously for the elections, after which they can be considered
 bina shart thama congress kaa haathcongress main shaamil hue jogendra singh awana ne kaha, jahaan tak mantri pad kaa sawaal he, yah faisla mukhyamantri, pradesh prabharee or congress adhyaksh kaa he
 We will work to win the Congress party firmly
 unhone kaha ki ham bina kisi shart ke congress main aae hai
 Let us know that the civic elections to be held this month are considered to be important according to the politics of Rajasthan after the assembly by-elections held last month
 mana ja rahaa he ki pichley maheene hue vidhansabha upachunaavon ke nateezon se congress kii ummid nikaay chunaavon ko lekar kaaphi badi he
 Significantly, the Congress candidate won the Mandawa Assembly by-election by over 30,000 votes and defeated the BJP candidate
 jabaki khinvsar ke upachunaav main rashtriya loktantric party ke ummidavaar se congress pratyaashee ko kariban 4500 voton se haar mili thi
 The state elections are to be held on November 16, the result of which will come on November 19
 CAA Protests: naagarikta sanshodhan kanoon (citizenship Amendment Act) ko lekar purvottar rajyon ke saath-saath jamiya millia islamia university (jamia Millia Islamia) or aligarh muslim university (aligarh Muslim University) sahit desh kii kai jane-maane vishvavidhyalayon ke chaatr pradarshan par utar aae hai
 In Jamia Millia Islamia last night, the case caught fire when police brutalized protesting students
 is maamle ko dekhte hue bollywood kalakaar bhi lagaataar apana twit kar rahe hai
 Recently, Bollywood actress Pooja Bhatt has also tweeted on this issue, in which Pooja Bhatt said that India is burning
 To speak with silence when we should protest is what makes cowards out of men
 India is burning
 One can't be mute anymore
 Actress Pooja Bhatt gave her reaction by tweeting on the atmosphere being created in the country
 unka yah twit soshal media par jamkar viral ho rahaa he, saath hi log isapar khub coment bhi kar rahe hai
 Pooja Bhatt wrote in her tweet, "when we should have protested then we are keeping silence, this thing has kept us coward
 bharat jal rahaa he
 Now one cannot remain calm
 " puja bhatta ke is twit par log khub riection de rahe hai
 Let us know that Pooja Bhatt is very much in the news about her tweets
 itnaa hi nahin, apane twits ke jariye vah aksar samasamyik muddon par bhi bakhubi raay pesh karte hai
 Explain that after the demonstrations of the students of Jamia University and Aligarh Muslim University against the Citizenship Amendment Act, the students of Lucknow's Darul Uloom Nadwatul University also got a strong demonstration
 is pradarshan ke dauraan chaatro or police ke bich jhadap hone kii bhi soochna he
 However, the situation is now being told as normal
 vahiin, aligarh, saharanpur or meerut sahit upi ke kai jilon main internet seva band kar di gai he
 As the results of the Kairana Lok Sabha and Nurpur assembly by-elections became a question of prestige for the Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP), the party's infighting came to the surface
 bijanour ke saansad bhaaratendu singh ne chunaav prabharee or panchayat raaj mantri bhupendra choudhary ko nishane par le liya
 Bharatendu Singh said, "there should be some people who have experience in winning elections
 bhupendra singh teen baar chunaav haare, unhen pradesh sarkaar main panchayat raaj mantri bana diya gaya
 "sangeet Som, an MLA from Sardhana (meerut) who was the flag bearer of bjp's Hindutva agenda in western UP, also did not sit silent
 ve bole, "kairana loksabhaa upachunaav main bhaajapa kii haar kii ek vajah sthaneey janpratinidhiyon se janata kii naaraazgi he
 Shyam Prakash, MLA from Gopamau, Hardoi, lashed out at the state government and the organization after the defeat
 pichley dinon mukhyamantri yogi adityanath ko nirih bataane vaale shyamprakash ne fasebuk par likhaa, "modi naam se paa gaye raaj, kar na sake janata man kaaj, sangh sanghathan haath lagaam, mukhyamantri bhi asahaay
 The BJP, which had described the over-confident as the reason for the defeat in the Gorakhpur and Phulpur Lok Sabha by-elections, had given full force to feed the lotus in the by-elections in Kairana and Noorpur
 magar haar ne party ko agle varsh hone vaale loksabhaa chunaav kii taiyaariyon ko aainaa dikhaa diya he
 The defeat in Kairana and Nurpur bypolls may be attributed to BJP state president Mahendra Nath Pandey not being in favor of local equations (see conversation) but the reality is that the saffron party has suffered the brunt of lack of coordination among the leaders
 kairana loksabhaa upachunaav main chunaav sanchaalan main prantiy netaaon kii bhoomika ko lekar bhaajapa netritv ne padtaal shuru kii he
 For a long time there has been discontent within the party over a provincial leader of the BJP
 nurpur vidhansabha upachunaav main bhi bhaajapa ke kai netaaon par bhitarghaat kaa aarope he
 Allegedly, these leaders did not want any political member of their family to remain in existence after the death of Lokendra Pratap Singh
 banaras hindu vishvavidhyalay (biechayu) ke samaaj shaastra vibhaag main professor dow
 Ajit Kumar explains, "on the one hand, while opposite-minded parties are forgetting differences and forming alliances against the BJP, on the other hand, mutual dissatisfaction among BJP leaders at the local level is weakening the party
 ''varchasv kii jangsthaneey str par bhaajapa netaaon ke bich varchasv kii jang ne bhi party ke bhitari anushaasan ko nuksaan pahunchaaya he
 During the cooperative elections, BJP MLA Yogesh Verma's district cooperative election in-charge Shyam Pandey and MLA Ramkumar Verma were estranged to make Vineet Mannar, the nephew of former SP MLA in Lakhimpur, during the election
 lakhimpur ke vikaas bhawan main 15 janvari kii der shaam donon netaaon kii maujuudagi main unke samarthakon main laat-ghunse chale
 Questions are also being raised on the attitude of the state government

" ‚Äô Vishwa Hindu Parishad's International President Ashok Singhal has simultaneously targeted the Maharashtra ATS and Congress investigating the Malegaon blasts

 tunda, lashkar-e-taiyaba (eliti) kaa sheersh aatankwaadi he, tathaa anderworld don daaud ibrahim kaa sahyogi he
 Friday around 3 pm Tunda
 00 baje nepal seemaa ke najadik uttarakhand ke banbasa ilaake se giraftaar kiya gaya
 He was produced in a Delhi court on Saturday
 adaalat ne tunda ko teen dinon ke liye police hiraasat main bhej diya
 Special Commissioner of Delhi Police SN Srivastava said, "A Pakistani passport has been recovered from him, whose number is 'AC 4413161'
 yah passport 23 janvari ko abdul kuddus naam se jari kiya gaya tha
 " police ne bataaya ki tunda desh main vibhinn aapraadhik maamalon main vaanchit he or desh ke sheersh 20 ati vaanchit aatankwaadiyon kii suchi main shaamil he
 Tunda is wanted in 21 terrorist cases in 1994, 1996 and 1998 in Delhi
 shrivastav ne bataaya, "tunda, lashkar-e-taiyaba tathaa pakistani khufia agency iesai se kareeb se judaa rahaa he
 " uttar pradesh ke gajiabad jile ke pilkhua se taalluk rakhana vaala tunda bam banane kaa visheshgy he tathaa 1985 main mumbai main bam banane ke dauraan visphot ho jane ke kaaran uskaa baanyaa haath ud gaya tha
 Since then, he was nicknamed 'tunda'
 daaud kaa sahyogi tunda eliti kaa bam visheshgy aatankwaadi tha, tathaa 1993 main mumbai main hue shrunkhalabaddh bam visphoton, dilli main 1997-98 main hue bam visphoton tathaa uttar pradesh main hue shrunkhalabaddh bam visphoton ke alaava punjab tathaa haryana bam visphoton main kathith taur par shaamil tha
 Born in 1943 at Daryaganj in central Delhi, Tunda is also wanted in cases of serial bomb blasts in trains in Hyderabad, Gulbarga, Surat and Lucknow
 vah akele gajiabad main 13 aapraadhik ghatnaon main sanlipt rahaa he
 He has also reportedly worked with Hafiz Saeed, Zakiur Rehman Lakhvi, Wadhwa Singh, Ratandeep Singh, fugitive terrorist Abdul Aziz alias Bada Sajid of Karachi-based Indian Mujahideen and other terrorists
 tunda, patni sahit 1992 tak apane gaanv pilkhua main rahaa
 Police said that Tunda traded carpentry, scrap and clothing until he was 40 before becoming a hardcore jihadist terrorist
 police ne bataaya ki 1992 main babari masjid dhahaae jane ke turant baad tunda ne mumbai main ek kattarpanthi sanghathan kii sthapana kii
 Police further said that in January 1994, Tunda fled to Bangladesh, where he started training jihadis to make bombs in the capital Dhaka
 tippaniyan Two Bangladeshi disciples of Tunda - tamo-ur-rahman and Akbar alias Haroon - were arrested in February 1998 from Sadar Bazar railway station in Delhi
 baad main police ne aatankwaadi samooh ke 24 anya sadasyon ko bhi giraftaar kar liya tha
 For the past few years, Tunda had remained silent and investigators thought he was dead
 sarkaar ne 2008 main mumbai hamale (26 / 11) ke baad jab pakistan sarkaar ko ati vaanchit 20 aatankwaadiyon kii suchi saunpi to usamen tunda kaa naam pramukh aatankwaadiyon main shaamil tha
